# Task Board

Date: 2026-06-09

## Mainline Ownership

- [x] Codex is current development mainline / control tower.
- [x] Active branch: `codex/a21-air-mainline-control`
- [x] Product direction synced: StackChan is a bodily voice satellite / desktop Agent terminal, not an ESP32-hosted full brain.
- [x] Cloud-first runtime synced: production service runs in cloud; serial is dev/admin/recovery only.
- [x] Voice principle synced: copy xiaozhi audio/protocol semantics; own only the server side.
- [x] 5080lab mirror path synced: use it for domestic mirrors, large artifacts, dependency/container/model pulls.
- [x] ECS and StackChan firmware availability synced: both are available for gated preflight, fixture capture and evidence runs; production claims still require fresh gate output.

## Current Control Setup

- [x] 资料清单：`STACKCHAN_XIAOZHI_TOOLING_INVENTORY.md`
- [x] 服务端实施计划：`docs/superpowers/plans/2026-06-06-stackchan-xiaozhi-server.md`
- [x] 项目控制文档：`docs/control/*`
- [x] 本地忽略规则：`.gitignore`
- [x] 控制检查入口：`Makefile`

## Server Capability Audit

本节是当前真实状态，不是愿景。除非代码、测试、gate 和看板同时更新，否则不能在状态汇报里把未完成能力说成已完成。

| Capability | Status | Current Evidence / Gap |
|---|---|---|
| Xiaozhi-compatible voice runtime | Partial | Gateway WebSocket now enters `session.VoiceLoop`, handles `hello` / `listen` / `abort` / MCP / binary Opus, and mock simulator suite passes including the StackChan/Xiaozhi `asr_final_without_listen_stop` child and MCP bridge-skip feedback child. The public Xiaozhi OTA config endpoint can provision official firmware with cloud WebSocket URL/token/version only after `Device-Id` and `Client-Id` match configured hardware. `device-provisioning-check` gives a token-gated, non-VoiceLoop pre-capture check for URL/identity/hello readiness. A21 Air ECS dev runtime is live behind Caddy, public OTA returns the expected redacted shape for the configured StackChan and 403 for unknown hardware, and `stackchan-sim --scenario hello_only` passes against the public WebSocket through the 5080lab domestic egress. Real no-stop ECS simulator with the hardware fixture now passes, proving StackChan can send `listen/start` plus audio without a client `listen/stop` and still receive TTS through provider ASR final. |
| Default real voice profile | Partial | Default config is `siliconflow-dashscope-voice` with DashScope ASR/TTS + SiliconFlow LLM, and `voice-profile-check` guards non-mock profile/model selection. ECS 20-run real-fixture provider evidence passed on 2026-06-07 after decoding Xiaozhi raw Opus to PCM for DashScope ASR: DashScope ASR 20/20 first transcript p50/p95 303/429 ms and total p50/p95 1016/1732 ms; SiliconFlow LLM 20/20 first token p50/p95 124/258 ms and total p50/p95 139/285 ms; DashScope TTS 20/20 first audio p50/p95 489/649 ms and total p50/p95 1041/1478 ms. A later physical no-audio failure was traced to DashScope TTS provider bytes being passed through as Xiaozhi Opus; the deployed hotfix requests provider PCM and encodes 60 ms frames through libopus into Xiaozhi raw Opus, and user retest confirmed real device audio playback recovered. VoiceLoop now avoids sending very short comma lead-ins as standalone TTS segments and handles ASCII sentence punctuation for faster non-Chinese punctuation first-speech; DashScope TTS volume/rate/pitch can be tuned through safe env overrides without code changes. A 2026-06-08 mature ASR/LLM/TTS state-machine review added focused regression coverage and fixes so barge-in sends old `tts/stop` before provider profile resolve can block, TTS provider failure after `tts/start` still closes the device state with `tts/stop` plus idle cues, and trace-backed `tts_stop_sent.fields.stop_latency_ms` captures cancel-to-stop latency for physical barge-in acceptance. This proves the default real voice profile gate on ECS plus the critical physical playback path; fallback matrix/evidence archive and final physical acceptance remain separate gates. |
| Provider compatibility adapters | Partial | Implemented and fixture-tested: DashScope ASR/LLM/TTS, Doubao ASR/LLM/TTS, SiliconFlow LLM, Moonshot LLM, StepFun LLM, MiniMax LLM/TTS, DeepSeek LLM, Anthropic LLM. SiliconFlow, DashScope, DeepSeek, Moonshot, MiniMax, Doubao/Ark and StepFun LLM adapters now send OpenAI-compatible function tool schemas and parse streaming `tool_calls` deltas into complete tool calls. Deployed source ref `7bd9aafd28f1` makes voice-path LLM request builders consume normalized structured `system`/`user` messages when present and keep bounded short-output controls where supported: SiliconFlow `max_tokens:160`, DashScope `max_completion_tokens:160` with `enable_thinking:false`, MiniMax `max_completion_tokens:160` with M3 `thinking.type:"disabled"`, Doubao `max_completion_tokens:160` with `thinking.type:"disabled"`, DeepSeek `max_tokens:160` with `thinking.type:"disabled"`, StepFun `max_tokens:160`, and Moonshot `max_completion_tokens:160`. Current mainline is Alibaba + ByteDance first, with MiniMax/DeepSeek/Kimi as already-implemented backups; Tencent Hunyuan/TokenHub must stay research/backlog unless explicitly requested, not a provider-development priority. Not implemented: GLM, Baidu Qianfan/ERNIE, Tencent Hunyuan/TokenHub, Baichuan, SenseNova, Yi. |
| Runtime provider hot switching | Partial | VoiceLoop resolves a provider profile at each `listen/start`; admin API can list a safe profile catalog plus effective device statuses, and can GET/PUT/DELETE per-device overrides; auto fallback can switch after configured consecutive yellow/error turns, but Inner Test 1 keeps it disabled until full ASR/LLM/TTS fallback evidence exists. The safe catalog marks fallback profiles that share default ASR/TTS and only swap LLM via `shared_default_voice_io` / `llm_only_fallback`, supporting review of the DashScope LLM rollback path without enabling automatic fallback. Live ECS profile checks pass for both default `siliconflow-dashscope-voice` and manual/admin fallback candidate `dashscope-cosyvoice`. |
| Personality / persona layer | Partial | Persona YAML loader, prompt policy and VoiceLoop LLM context builder are implemented. Current voice path still outputs speakable text only; structured JSON response parsing is deferred to tool orchestration. Current ECS source ref `071867ae553f` strengthens the voice prompt contract for Chinese spoken turns: default to short speakable Chinese, no JSON/tool text in spoken output, and explicit continuity behavior for elliptical follow-ups. |
| Memory / preferences | Partial | Memory taxonomy, MemoryStore interface, SQLite persistent repository, ignored runtime DB path, prompt injection, high-precision explicit transcript writeback, private admin memory list/upsert/delete, deterministic profile-summary compaction and a scoped read-only `memory.lookup` service tool are implemented. Short-turn dialogue continuity is controlled by `agent.recent_turns`; when `agent.memory_db_path` is configured, successful voice turns now persist bounded current-device user text plus actually spoken assistant text in a separate SQLite `recent_turns` table, so restarts/deploys keep short context without polluting long-term `memories`; when no memory DB is configured, the gateway falls back to the bounded in-memory recent-turn store. Private admin can now inspect the same bounded recent-turn store for one explicit device through `/internal/v1/recent-turns`, making continuity failures directly diagnosable without reading raw DB files or public routes. Current ECS source ref `4b64da997bfb` renders recent turns in Chinese voice-context labels, instructs the model to resolve “继续/那下一步呢/刚才那个/这个/它/三件事” style follow-ups from recent dialogue before answering, and makes physical acceptance metrics/report/validator require safe `llm_request.fields.recent_turn_count` evidence through `llm_request_turns`, `llm_recent_context_turns`, `max_recent_turn_count` and `continuity_context_ok`, without exposing prompt or transcript text. A 2026-06-09 read-only ECS check (`t-sh06ncjyqaxihvk`, corrected admin check `t-sh06nck12xhob9c`) confirmed the live runtime has `agent.memory_db_path=/var/lib/a21-air/memory/stackchan-memory.sqlite3`, `agent.recent_turns=8`, recent LLM requests carrying `recent_turn_count=8`, and eight stored recent turns for device `44:1b:f6:e2:74:50`. Deployed source ref `57e7961755ca` now separates current-session recent dialogue from older cross-session device references, while treating the only available previous-connection turns as continuity after reconnect. Deployed source ref `290b4b111590` sends persona/memory/continuity instructions as the provider `system` message, recent turns as alternating `user`/`assistant` chat-history messages, and the ASR final transcript as the current `user` message, while preserving legacy prompt text for safe length/fallback metadata. Physical retest `server/var/runtime/hardware/serial/stackchan-continuity-two-turn-20260609-1142.log` now proves basic spoken two-turn continuity on the real unit, and ECS trace invoke `t-sh06ne2wrizfaww` showed the follow-up request carried `recent_turn_count=8` and structured `message_count=4`. Advanced semantic/LLM curation remains future work. |
| Agent bridge compatibility | Partial | `server/internal/agents` now defines cloud-side bridge boundaries: router modes, V21 professional-only blocking, V21 `/internal/v1/knowledge/voice-query` client, OpenClaw/Hermes text-for-gateway-TTS bridges, and Claude/Hermes/OpenClaw tool-intent to gateway-owned tool-call conversion with bridge-boundary filtering. Empty/unknown tool names and nested `v21.voice_query` intents are dropped before VoiceLoop sees them; Hermes/OpenClaw can restrict forwarded tool intents through per-bridge `allowed_tool_intents` allowlists and `max_tool_intents` caps from 0 to the hard limit of two, and forwarded calls still pass through the gateway orchestrator before side effects. Hermes/OpenClaw runtime routes can also be capped per bridge/device through `max_runtime_routes_per_minute`, runtime transcript input can be capped through `max_runtime_input_chars`, and consecutive runtime errors can trigger a per bridge/device `max_runtime_errors_before_cooldown` / `runtime_error_cooldown_ms` cooldown; capped, over-limit or cooled-down turns do not call the external bridge, record only safe `agent_route_skipped` trace metadata (`reason`, `mode`, `destination`) and fall back to the normal LLM path. Empty OpenClaw/Hermes responses with no safe tool calls do not mark the turn handled, so VoiceLoop falls back to the normal LLM path instead of speaking a meaningless acknowledgement. OpenClaw/Hermes runtime errors record only a safe `agent_route_error` code and fall back to the normal LLM path unless the turn context itself was canceled. Runtime agent mode is device-scoped; private admin can list the safe mode catalog plus effective device statuses, can GET/PUT/DELETE per-device mode overrides, and the public router now also exposes device-auth `/xiaozhi/device-mode/status` plus `/xiaozhi/device-mode/select` so the current StackChan can switch AI.Agent/Hermes/OpenClaw/Professional launcher state without holding an admin token or injecting a voice turn. The device endpoint accepts only configured mode ids, rejects request-body device ids by unknown-field validation, authenticates with `Device-Id`, `Client-Id` and raw/Bearer device token, and returns only safe `active_mode`, `requested_mode`, `available` and `reason` state. Selecting the configured default mode through the device endpoint clears the override, so a return-to-daily launcher action does not leave sticky state. Its non-casual availability is now sourced from the same runtime-status view used by admin/VoiceLoop: roleplay checks Hermes, tool checks OpenClaw, and professional checks V21, so selecting a disabled bridge returns safe `bridge_disabled` instead of a false healthy UI state. Private admin can list the safe V21/Hermes/OpenClaw bridge catalog with enabled state, required mode, invocation type, service-tool name, bounded-output/tool-intent flags, safe allowed tool-intent names, bounded max tool-intent caps, bounded runtime route/input/error-cooldown caps and boolean fallback policy flags, and can inspect per-device bridge availability reasons through `/internal/v1/agent-runtime-status`, including dynamic `runtime_rate_limited`, `runtime_input_too_long` and `runtime_error_cooldown` reasons when the shared runtime router would skip the external bridge. The status route remains read-only and does not execute bridges or expose URLs, env names, token values or provider error bodies. `v21.voice_query` is registered only when `agent.v21.enabled=true` and executes only when that device is in professional mode. VoiceLoop now recognizes explicit natural-language professional-mode/roleplay-mode/tool-mode entry/exit commands after ASR final, updates the device mode store, speaks a TTS confirmation, and skips LLM/memory writeback for those control turns. When `agent.openclaw.enabled=true`, tool mode routes ASR text to OpenClaw, speaks the returned text through gateway TTS, and sends allowed returned tool intents through the gateway orchestrator. When `agent.hermes.enabled=true`, roleplay mode routes ASR text to Hermes with the same TTS/orchestrator boundary. Richer agent policies remain future work. Claude also remains available as a direct LLM provider adapter. |
| LLM-driven tool calls | Partial | VoiceLoop now consumes provider-emitted `chunk.ToolCalls`, executes them through a server-owned MCP/tool orchestrator, can dispatch registered gateway service tools through an explicit permission boundary, records safe trace metadata, and keeps speakable text on TTS without waiting for tool results. Concrete service tools now include scoped `memory.lookup`, optional allowlisted `homeassistant.get_state`, optional allowlisted `homeassistant.call_action` with operator-configured numeric/string/boolean slots, optional internal-adapter `search.web`, optional allowlisted `feishu.list_targets` / `feishu.send_text`, optional local `reminder.announce`, optional `camera.request_capture` confirmation request, optional semantic `stackchan.express`, optional bounded `stackchan.expression_sequence` body/display cues with operator-configured cue policies, optional configured `stackchan.play_expression_sequence` preset ids for operator-owned body/display macros, and optional professional-mode gated `v21.voice_query`. `v21.voice_query` is hidden from provider-facing `LLMRequest.Tools` outside professional mode while the execution-time service-tool guard remains in place. Provider-facing raw/low-value StackChan MCP tools (`self.get_device_status`, `self.robot.set_head_angles`, `self.robot.set_led_color`, `self.screen.set_scene`) and `self.camera.take_photo` are no longer exposed to or executable from the voice hot path by default; `camera.request_capture` is config-gated under `tools.camera.enabled`, returns only `requires_confirmation:true` with bounded reason character count, does not call hardware, does not return an image and does not expose the reason text in the tool result. Deployed source ref `53c468f9e2b3` also makes model-driven StackChan body expression tools opt-in through `stackchan.expression.provider_tools_enabled`; the live ECS config currently has `provider_tools_enabled=false`, so casual voice turns keep official StackChan body behavior plus server-owned lifecycle LED/display feedback without letting the model trigger extra head/LED sequences. Private admin can list the registered service-tool catalog with name, description, permission, allow/permission status and filtered schema property names without executing tools, and the public xiaozhi router does not mount that catalog. VoiceLoop passes provider-safe aliases for available service/MCP tool schemas into `LLMRequest`, maps aliases back to internal tool names before execution, and tool-only LLM responses can get one bounded follow-up LLM request with tool results and operator-controlled `tools.tool_followup` enable/positive max-results/max-bytes/allowed-tools policy. If a tool-only turn executes only tools whose results are not allowed or useful for the follow-up prompt, VoiceLoop now sends one no-tools recovery LLM request that asks for a short spoken answer or confirmation instead of ending silently. By default the follow-up has no recursive tool schemas; when `allow_tool_calls=true`, only already-exposed `allowed_tools` schemas are passed into that second request, execution is filtered again after alias resolution, `max_tool_calls` is capped, and the final answer request carries no tools. Example config allows only voice-safe read tools (`memory.lookup`, `homeassistant.get_state`, `search.web`) into the result prompt and leaves recursive follow-up tool calls disabled. OpenAI-compatible tool schema/streaming parser coverage exists for SiliconFlow, DashScope, DeepSeek, Moonshot, MiniMax, Doubao/Ark and StepFun. Still pending: actual camera capture/stream mode with user-visible confirmation, Feishu read/search/document tools, calendar tools, richer multi-step agent policies and arbitrary HA service passthrough beyond configured actions/slots. |
| StackChan body/display/LED scheduling | Partial | Gateway semantic screen scenes and body tools are implemented with simulator gates, but the physical default is now conservative because official StackChan V1.4.1 already has its own avatar/body behavior. `stackchan.body.listen_start_motion_enabled` defaults to false, the example min command gap is now 320 ms, the per-turn command cap is 6, and automatic `stackchan.expression.event_cues` are disabled by default; simulator/app tests explicitly enable these cues only when proving the tool chain. ECS runtime config was patched to the same conservative policy after deploy (`min_command_gap_ms:320`, `max_commands_per_turn:6`, `listen_start_motion_enabled:false`, `event_cues:{}`), then restarted with `voice-profile-check`, `/healthz` and `/readyz` passing. The current physical firmware is the 2026-06-09 `1445` speaking-only wake/barge-in artifact, which supersedes the `1245` mode-launcher artifact while preserving official-lifecycle launcher AI.Agent, single-`da tou`, hot WebSocket, hot-channel wake, voice-always-awake, head-touch debounce, calm motion and A21.MODE; the rejected launcher-loop runtime-start artifact and rejected `1435` all-state wake artifact must not be used. Voice turns still dispatch ordered display lifecycle scenes through a nonblocking FIFO path when `self.screen.set_scene` exists, and ordered lifecycle LEDs remain listening green, thinking amber, speaking blue and idle off through `stackchan.body.lifecycle_leds`. Lifecycle scene captions, emotions, accents and motion hints are configurable under `stackchan.display.lifecycle_scenes`; agent-mode, tool-running, tool-succeeded/tool-failed, Home Assistant state/action, search, memory-updated, camera-capturing, reminder-due, agent-route and policy-skipped agent-route display triggers are configurable under `stackchan.display.event_scenes`; these policy maps are validated before startup. The real StackChan firmware currently did not expose `self.screen.set_scene` in MCP, so gateway display scene dispatch now requires both allowlist permission and actual discovered tool availability before calling it; official xiaozhi ASR/LLM/TTS text display still works through the normal firmware path, while A21.MODE uses a separate top-level app UI for mode switching. Private admin can inspect a safe display-scene catalog with effective lifecycle/event scene ids, scene/emotion/accent/motion metadata, caption-presence flags, display bounds and per-device screen availability, without exposing captions or MCP method names. Model tool calls can use `stackchan.express` semantic cues (`attentive`, `nod`, `celebrate`, `thinking`, `settle`), `stackchan.expression_sequence` sequences of one to three fixed cues, and `stackchan.play_expression_sequence` configured preset ids. The gateway maps all of them to bounded head, LED and screen commands after validating cue lists before dispatch and pacing cue dispatch through the `BodyScheduler` min-gap; operator-owned `stackchan.expression.cues` can override only fixed cue policies with validated motion, LED and scene fields, and `stackchan.expression.sequences` can define reusable preset cue macros without exposing cue lists, yaw/pitch, LED values or captions to the model. Private admin can inspect safe expression-sequence and expression-cue catalogs without exposing cue lists, captions or MCP method names. Model tool calls can also use `stackchan.show_card` when `stackchan.display.cards` is configured and the device exposes screen MCP; the provider sees only configured card IDs, optional captions are accepted only for cards with `allow_caption=true`, and captions are bounded before the SceneComposer sends `self.screen.set_scene`. Optional `stackchan.expression.lifecycle_cues` and `stackchan.expression.event_cues` remain operator opt-in body/LED feedback only; screen lifecycle/events remain owned by the ordered display queue and `stackchan.display.*_scenes`. Safe trace events now record StackChan body dispatch and lifecycle/event expression-cue dispatch outcomes without RGB values, yaw/pitch values, raw arguments, transcripts, prompts, generated text or token values. Official V1.4.1 parity caveat: the simulator body/display gates are mock gateway gates rather than complete firmware emulation, official LED payload names are now enforced as `red`/`green`/`blue` in gateway and simulator tests, and official V1.4.1 tools/list does not include `self.screen.set_scene` unless custom firmware or a separate StackChan app/avatar WS mapping adds it. Physical LED lifecycle retest, `大头` hot-channel wake retest, long-idle wake retest, passive touch/motion audit, mode-launcher boot, speaking-time barge-in and final fresh 20-turn physical acceptance passed on the real unit. Richer adaptive body behavior beyond conservative opt-in cues remains future work. |
| Home Assistant / local tools / search / Feishu / camera / calendar | Partial | Optional `homeassistant.get_state` is implemented as a read-only service tool using the Home Assistant REST states API, gated by config, token env and an entity allowlist; payloads expose only safe state fields. Optional `homeassistant.call_action` can call only operator-configured action IDs whose domain, service and entity IDs are fixed in config; service data may include static values plus operator-defined slots with validated string, number, integer or boolean values. Optional `search.web` calls an operator-owned internal search adapter via URL/token env, returns bounded result summaries and can filter to configured bare domains. Optional local `reminder.announce` can acknowledge a currently due reminder with bounded title/message inputs, no external calls and no full-message echo in the tool result. Optional Feishu tools can list configured voice-safe targets; voice-runtime `feishu.send_text` now returns a safe confirmation request without Feishu HTTP, while `feishu-smoke` provides the repeatable operator real-send command and prints only target/message-id. Optional `camera.request_capture` is a server-side confirmation gate only: it is disabled by default, accepts a bounded reason, returns no reason text/image, and never invokes StackChan camera MCP. Actual receive IDs live in env and do not appear in tool payloads. Arbitrary model-supplied HA domain/service/entity/target/data passthrough, actual camera capture/stream execution, Feishu user-confirmed send flow, Feishu read/search/document tools, calendar and other local service implementations are not registered yet. |
| ECS runtime packaging | Partial | `ecs-package` now generates a safe Aliyun ECS/systemd runtime wrapper with `stackchan-gateway.service`, `preflight.sh`, `gateway.env.example`, `README.md` and `manifest.json`; it derives required env names from the configured default voice profile, rejects dirty output directories, and writes no binary, config copy, provider env file or secret values. `ecs-package-validate` validates the fixed file set, manifest/unit/preflight alignment, empty env-template values and secret-like content patterns. `ecs-preflight-dry-run` validates a generated package plus a private runtime env file/config/default voice profile without starting systemd or running provider network probes, and rejects group/world-readable env files. Actual ECS startup preflight has passed through systemd with the private cloud env, and source-backed actual-host release-package dry-run now passes with source ref `42037f3efb21` / `clean`. |
| ECS production deployment | Partial | A21 Air cloud dev runtime is deployed independently under `/opt/a21-air`, listens on localhost service/admin/metrics ports, and Caddy proxies public 80/443 to the gateway. This is still not wider production promotion until the inner-test package is frozen and the fallback/rollback policy is explicitly selected. |

| Acoustic quality capture | Partial | Local USB measurement-mic capture tooling now exists as `acoustic-devices` and `acoustic-capture`. It lists macOS audio devices through `system_profiler`, captures ECM999U/avfoundation WAV through ffmpeg or analyzes an existing PCM16 WAV, and writes a manifest with sample rate, channels, duration, peak dBFS, RMS dBFS, clipped percent, silence percent and DC offset. The tool refuses repository output paths that are not ignored by git so raw WAV files do not become commit candidates. ECS TTS tuning now has a fixed Cloud Assistant helper, `server/deploy/aliyun/tts-tuning-update.sh`, for safe dry-run/status and bounded DashScope TTS volume/rate/pitch/model/voice plus Opus downlink bitrate/complexity env updates. It backs up `/etc/a21-air/gateway.env`, runs `voice-profile-check`, restarts systemd and checks ECS-local health/readiness without printing secrets. Baseline captures now exist: quiet idle ECM999U capture recorded peak `-37.23 dBFS`, RMS `-50.25 dBFS`, `clipped_percent=0`, `dc_offset=-0.000036`; post-voice-always-awake TTS capture recorded peak `-21.89 dBFS`, RMS `-44.48 dBFS`, `clipped_percent=0`, `dc_offset=-0.000002`. This points away from service-side clipping/DC and toward device amp/power/placement/voice tuning for any remaining slight electrical feel; it does not alter Xiaozhi sample rates, binary frame version or the ASR/LLM/TTS state machine, and does not replace final real-device barge-in/Wi-Fi/restart acceptance. |

## Current Voice Experience Debt

- [x] Continuous conversation/context: basic physical two-turn continuity now passes. The live ECS path persists bounded recent turns in SQLite `recent_turns`, injects them into structured provider messages, and the real unit answered a follow-up from immediate prior context in `server/var/runtime/hardware/serial/stackchan-continuity-two-turn-20260609-1142.log`: after `请记住，我喜欢喝蓝莓乌龙茶。`, the tail follow-up `我刚才说我喜欢喝什么？` was answered as `您喜欢喝蓝莓乌龙茶呀！`. Read-only ECS trace invoke `t-sh06ne2wrizfaww` showed the follow-up LLM request carried safe context metadata `recent_turn_count=8` and `message_count=4`. Richer long-term memory/personality quality remains normal product tuning, not a missing voice-chain capability.
- [ ] Audio quality: physical feedback says playback has a slight electrical/current feel. Keep Xiaozhi Opus semantics intact; do not replace the proven PCM -> libopus -> Xiaozhi raw Opus path. Current ECS source ref `a8175f89061f` supports bounded Opus downlink bitrate/complexity tuning while keeping defaults at `64 kbps`, complexity `10`, voice signal, VBR enabled, DTX/FEC off. On 2026-06-09 ECS tuning invoke `t-sh06ncppit1dds0` lowered `DASHSCOPE_TTS_VOLUME` from `42` to `36` and passed `voice-profile-check`, `/healthz` and `/readyz`; post-deploy status invoke `t-sh06ncqtv31nocg` confirmed volume `36` and Opus bitrate/complexity still default. Source PCM traces and ECM999U captures now show no clipping/DC issue: quiet idle capture was peak `-37.23 dBFS`, RMS `-50.25 dBFS`, `clipped_percent=0`, `dc_offset=-0.000036`; TTS capture was peak `-21.89 dBFS`, RMS `-44.48 dBFS`, `clipped_percent=0`, `dc_offset=-0.000002`. Remaining work is physical listening A/B around power, placement, device volume/gain and voice choice, not a protocol rewrite.
- [x] Motion naturalness baseline: physical feedback says gateway motion can feel unnatural and may conflict with official StackChan preset/autonomous motion. Default gateway motion is now conservative: no listen-start head pose unless explicitly enabled, larger command gap, lower per-turn cap, no automatic event body cues, no default `self.robot.set_head_angles` device MCP exposure, no provider-facing/executable raw StackChan head/LED/screen MCP tools in voice hot path, no default Hermes/OpenClaw `stackchan.express` tool-intent forwarding, and deployed source ref `53c468f9e2b3` hides semantic `stackchan.express` / `stackchan.expression_sequence` / `stackchan.play_expression_sequence` from provider-facing voice LLM requests unless `stackchan.expression.provider_tools_enabled=true`. Post-deploy status invoke `t-sh06ncqtv31nocg` confirmed live ECS has `provider_tools_enabled=false`, `listen_start_motion_enabled=false` and `event_cues_count=0`; passive serial audit `server/var/runtime/hardware/serial/stackchan-passive-motion-touch-audit-20260609-1200.log` saw zero touch, head-pet, servo or motion spam in 45 seconds. Future movement should be built as deliberate semantic micro-cues, not background motion.
- [x] Stale green/body state: 2026-06-08 acceptance attempt showed stale green LED after session close and body dispatch generation reuse; later 2026-06-09 smoke showed the official post-TTS auto-listen tail could stay green for more than 90 seconds without ASR final/close. Fixes now advance generation on idle auto-listen, send session-close LED-off cleanup synchronously, add a 10 second no-speech timeout only for post-TTS auto-listen tails, skip stale lifecycle LED requests after the active turn is gone, and delay post-speaking idle feedback so official continuous-listen does not flicker off then green. ECS now runs `4c69d57`, and physical serial retest `server/var/runtime/hardware/serial/stackchan-staged-dialog-tail-retest-20260609-1133.log` passed with green listening, blue speaking, green post-TTS tail, idle-off after timeout, no infinite green and no off->green flicker.

## Official V1.4.1 Parity Register

| Area | Current Gap | Mainline Action |
|---|---|---|
| LED MCP payload and lifecycle | Official `self.robot.set_led_color` uses `red`, `green`, `blue`; gateway and simulator now emit/expect those official argument names. Gateway lifecycle LED feedback is now ordered and configurable: listening green, thinking amber, speaking blue and idle off by default. | Code-level TDD gate passes for green/amber/blue/off sequence, safe trace redaction and generation anti-regression. | Screen MCP | Official StackChan V1.4.1 / xiaozhi v2.2.4 tools/list does not include `self.screen.set_scene`. | Keep display-scene dispatch gated by discovered tools; do not claim physical support unless custom firmware or `/stackChan/ws` mapping adds it. |
| Xiaozhi binary audio | Current live ECS config is still WebSocket version 1, but official xiaozhi supports binary v1/v2/v3. | Gateway parser/downlink encoder and simulator now support v1 raw Opus plus official v2/v3 wrapped Opus. Device handshake `Protocol-Version` must match configured `server.websocket_version`; `cmd/stackchan-sim --protocol-version <1|2|3>` must pass, and fresh physical/fixture evidence is required before promoting any non-v1 active version. |
| StackChan app/avatar WS | Official `/stackChan/ws?deviceType=StackChan` is separate from the xiaozhi voice WS and carries avatar/JPEG/motion/call/dance/camera stream/heartbeat frames. | Treat as a separate simulator/runtime track if avatar, camera stream, dance or app-level rendering enters scope. |
| MCP tools/list | Mock simulator tools/list remains a custom narrow happy path; official V1.4.1 behavior is available only when explicitly selecting the official profile. | Use `--firmware-profile official-v1.4.1` for physical-adjacent tools/list and body/LED prechecks; keep mock profile results as regression evidence only. |
| Camera | Official firmware exposes `self.camera.take_photo`, but gateway default voice hot path hides/rejects it after the surprise-photo incident. | Future camera ability needs an explicit camera mode/tool gate, rate limits and user-visible confirmation semantics. |
